à¤à¤¹à¤¾ à¤¥à¤¾: 26 March, 2014,  Since 1947 for 65 Years  nobody thought of bringing the money stays away in the Foreign Banks to the country. The Government has failed in its role for 65 Years. This Court feels that you have failed in your duty.
